All reads, no writes — plan writes still go through existing `plans/service.ts`. **Plans service extended** with requiredDocs persistence (createPlan + updatePlan + toPlan() read path). **Tests:** **10/10 so-planning green** (5 service: list with partial/unplanned classification + detail with per-line plans + NotFoundError + ValidationError on bad uuid + BOM aggregator rejection when no linked BOM; 5 routes: 200 list/detail + 401 no-user + 400 bad-uuid + 404 unknown SO). Cost / pc + Purchase Remarks. **Required QC Documents section** with red header 📋 + Add Document button + per-row name datalist (presets fall back to Dimensional Inspection Report / FAI / MTC / Surface Finish / Visual Inspection) + Mandatory/Optional dropdown + footer note ("Mandatory docs will block QC completion"). > Prior: 2026-05-21 (PL-5 Assembly Tracker shipped — **Phase B complete (5/5 slices)**. Final slice introduces 2 new tables per ADR-030: **`assembly_units`** (one row per assembled equipment unit; tracks serial, date, assembledBy, dispatched flag + date/by/remarks, deductions jsonb for read-only snapshot) + **`assembly_tracking`** (manual override per (so_id, child_item_code) for component readiness, used when the planner declares N pieces ready that stock doesn't reflect). Both tables CASCADE-delete from sales_orders. Migration `0025_phase8_assembly_units.sql` applied via `_apply_0025.mjs`. **Drizzle schema** additions in `apps/api/src/db/schema.ts` mirror the SQL. **Shared zod** `packages/shared/src/schemas/assembly.ts` — component row + unit row + rollup + tracker response + write inputs (markUnitAssembled, markUnitDispatched, setReadinessOverride). **API service** `apps/api/src/modules/assembly/service.ts` — 6 exports: (1) `getAssemblyTracker(soId)` — main aggregator. Fetches SO + BOM master + lines + per-child stock from item_stock_balances + assembly_tracking overrides + assembly_units. Per-component math: totalNeed = qtyPerSet × orderQty; autoReady = min(stock, totalNeed); final = max(autoReady, overrideQty); shortfall = max(0, totalNeed - final); enoughForUnits = floor(final / qtyPerSet); status = ready (final >= need) | enough_for_some (enoughForUnits > 0) | shortage. Rollup: canAssembleAdditional = min(enoughForUnits) clamped at balance; bottleneck = component with the lowest enoughForUnits; status = done (assembled >= orderQty) | assembling (assembled > 0) | ready (canAssemble > 0) | waiting. (2) `listAssemblies()` — all Equipment SOs with assembled / dispatched counters. Uses 3 batched Drizzle queries (SO headers → orderQty agg + assembled agg + BOM code lookup) joined in memory. (3) `markUnitAssembled(soId, input)` — inserts new unit, auto-increments unit_no via SELECT MAX, refuses to exceed orderQty (ConflictError), refuses non-Equipment SOs (ValidationError). (4) `markUnitDispatched(unitId, input)` — flips dispatched=true, refuses re-dispatch (ConflictError). (5) `undoLastUnit(soId)` — soft-deletes the latest non-deleted unit, refuses if it's already dispatched (caller must reverse dispatch first). (6) `setReadinessOverride(soId, childCode, input)` — upsert into assembly_tracking; reuses any soft-deleted row (un-deletes); resolves child_item_id from items master best-effort. **Routes** REST endpoints: GET /assemblies + GET /assemblies/:soId + POST /assemblies/:soId/units + PATCH /assemblies/units/:unitId/dispatch + DELETE /assemblies/:soId/units/last + PUT /assemblies/:soId/overrides/:childCode. **Defensive UUID filter** in listAssemblies: legacy dev DB has SO-DEMO-EQ with `bom_master_id='demo-bom-001'` (non-UUID stored in uuid column from pre-migration data); a regex filter on bomIds skips these rows from the BOM lookup so the query doesn't trip `invalid input syntax for type uuid`. **Tests: 20/20 green** (14 service + 6 routes). Fixture creates 1 Equipment SO + 1 line (orderQty 5) + 1 BOM with 2 child items (qty/set 1 and 2) + per-child stock balances (50 + 10 = enough for 5 units). Covers happy path readiness math, override max(auto, override) rule, full unit lifecycle assemble→dispatch→undo with conflict guards, listAssemblies, non-Equipment SO rejection. **Web module** `apps/web/src/modules/assembly/` — `useAssembliesList()` + `useAssemblyTracker(soId)` + 4 mutation hooks; `routes/list.tsx` showing all Equipment SOs with required/assembled/dispatched/status badge; `routes/detail.tsx` with header + 6-tile rollup strip (Required/Assembled/Dispatched/Balance/Can-assemble/Status) + bottleneck banner + components table with inline override edit + "Assemble next unit" form (serial + assembledBy inputs) + Undo last button (disabled when no units or latest is dispatched) + units table with per-row Dispatch button. **Sidebar** gets "🔧 Assembly Tracker" link in Planning dept. **Router** — 2 new routes (/assemblies + /assemblies/$soId). **All quality gates green:** api typecheck + lint clean; web typecheck + lint + build clean (index 1447 KB raw / 187 KB gzip, +38 KB from PL-4). **Full Phase B test surface: 112/112 green** (41 calc-engine + 9 so-status + 9 so-overview + 33 plans + 20 assembly). Phase B Planning module complete — 5/5 slices, ~10K LOC + 5 commits + 2 migrations + 7 new tables across the chain. Active task: pick next direction.)
> Prior: 2026-05-21 (PL-4 SO/JW Planning workflow shipped — fourth slice of Phase B per ADR-030. **No new schema** — uses the `plans` + `plan_ops` tables from PL-3. Two big additions to `apps/api/src/modules/plans/service.ts`: (1) **`getDefaultRouteOpsForItem(itemId, user)`** — finds the active route_card for an item, returns its ops formatted as `PlanOpInput[]` ready to splice into the plan form. OSP fields map: `route_card_ops.osp_vendor_id` → `plan_ops.outsource_vendor_id`, `route_card_ops.osp_vendor_code_text` → `plan_ops.outsource_vendor_text`, `route_card_ops.osp_lead_days` → `plan_ops.outsource_lead_days`. (2) **`executePlan(planId, user)`** — the planned → jc_created | pr_created transition. Single transaction with type-specific branches: **manufacture / assembly** → creates JC + copies plan_ops 1:1 → jc_ops, sets `plans.jc_id` + status='jc_created'; **direct_purchase** → creates 1 PR (linked via `sourceSoLineId` for cascade tracking), sets `plans.dp_pr_id` + status='pr_created'; **full_outsource** → creates a JW PR (operation='OUTSOURCE') + optionally a material PR when `fo_material_src` is set + not 'inhouse'/'self'/'in-house', sets `plans.fo_pr_id` (+ `plans.fo_mat_pr_id` if mat PR was created) + status='pr_created'. Code generators `nextPlanJcCode` (JC-PLN-<slug>-NN) + `nextPlanPrCode` (PR-DP-... / PR-FO-... / PR-FOMAT-...) follow the BOM cascade pattern. **Service-layer guards** — execute rejects non-planned plans (ValidationError); manufacture/assembly without ops fails before any write; FO without vendor/process fails; idempotency NOT required since each execute moves status forward (re-execute on jc_created returns the same error). **Dashboard `needsPlanning` KPI** wired in — single subquery joins sales_order_lines against plans NOT EXISTS where plan_status<>'cancelled' AND so/line both open. Closes the legacy "open SO lines with no plan" tile. **New routes:** POST /plans/:id/execute, GET /plans/default-ops?itemId=X. **Tests:** **11 new in service** + **3 new in routes** = **14 new** (PL-3 was 22, now 36); covers default-ops empty + populated + executePlan rejects non-planned + manufacture-creates-JC-and-copies-ops + dp-creates-PR + fo-creates-JW+mat-PR + fo-inhouse-skips-mat-PR + executePlan-no-ops-ValidationError. **Web module** `apps/web/src/modules/plans/` extended: (a) **`components/plan-form.tsx`** — shared form for new + edit (~530 LOC). Type picker disabled on edit per ADR-030 (changing type while planned would need re-validating fields). Conditional sections per type (DP shows vendor + cost; FO shows vendor + process + material + rate + delivery + cost-centre). Ops table only shown for manufacture/assembly. **"Load route card" button** wires `useDefaultRouteOps(itemId)` — only enabled when an itemId is set; replaces ops verbatim on click. (b) **`routes/new.tsx`** — uses the form for create + navigates to detail on success. (c) **`routes/edit.tsx`** — re-uses the form for edit; redirects to detail with a read-only banner if status is past 'planned'. PATCH payload mapped from the form-state shape. (d) **`routes/detail.tsx`** — reads plan, shows header (code + item + status badge + type icon), KV grid for header fields, type-specific section (DP/FO/manufacture), ops table. Actions: Finalize (in_planning only), Execute (planned only, type-specific button label), Edit (in_planning/planned only), Delete confirm flip (in_planning/planned only). (e) **`routes/list.tsx`** — full plan list with status/type/search filters + URL-state pagination (50/page). > Prior: 2026-05-21 (PL-1 SO Status Review shipped — first slice of Phase B Planning module per ADR-030. **calc-engine.ts** ported from legacy `calcEngine()` HTML L1626 as pure functions: `enrichOps` walks ops in seq order propagating `inputAvail` left→right; `rollupJC` derives 4-state JC status from enriched ops; `rollupSoLine` aggregates JCs into per-line `lineStatus`. **Ops status state machine** matches legacy verbatim (11 states): `complete`/`qc_pending`/`running`/`in_progress`/`available`/`waiting` for non-outsource, plus 5 outsource states `pending`/`pr_raised`/`po_created`/`at_vendor`/`received`. Prior: 2026-05-05 (T-051a follow-on #4 — emitter wired into **op-entry** as the natural substitute for "job-cards" in the queue. Discovery:`apps/api/src/modules/job-cards/service.ts`exposes only reads (listJobCards / getJobCard / countJobCards) — there is no createJobCard / updateJobCard / softDeleteJobCard service path; JC mutations happen via (a) migration, (b) op-entry cascade flipping status, (c) nc-register make_fresh cascade creating supplementary JCs. So the "job-cards" slot maps to **op-entry's three operator mutators**:`submitOpLog`→ OP_COMPLETE,`startOp`→ OP_START,`stopOp`→ OP_STOP. Action names + detail format mirror legacy`\_logActivity`calls (HTML L5459 / L5532 / L5704):`entity='Op'`(canonical short noun for filter dropdown — keeps cardinality low; legacy used per-op composite strings like "JC IN-XX-YY Op3" which would explode the dropdown),`refId=jc.code`, detail encodes `<jcCode> Op #<seq> — <verb> <qty>/<machine> by <operator>`. submitOpLog adds a small JC code lookup before the emit (loadJcOp returns jobCardId only). startOp / stopOp reuse their existing `meta`lookup. **Deferred to a separate commit:** cascade emissions for JC_COMPLETE + SO_CLOSED / SO_LINE_CLOSED / JW_CLOSED / JW_LINE_CLOSED that fire from`op-entry/sales-cascade.ts` when the last op closes — these need a design call about granularity (one JC_COMPLETE row vs also SO_CLOSED + line rows) and don't block the CRUD-emitter sweep. Also deferred: nc-register make_fresh cascade JC CREATE (will land naturally with the nc-register emitter). 1 new op-entry test (`emits OP_START / OP_STOP / OP_COMPLETE activity_log rows atomic with the mutation`) — uses a brand-new jc_op #99 to isolate from prior tests' running_ops residue, asserts entity/userId/userName + jcCode + Op #99 in detail. teardownFixture wipes activity_log by `refId LIKE 'T025-%'`. **api 24/24 green** in op-entry; workspace typecheck + lint + format clean. 5 modules remain: purchase-requests → purchase-orders → goods-receipt-notes → nc-register → delivery-challans, then op-entry cascade audit as a final follow-on.)

Prior: 2026-05-04 (Test-suite cleanup hygiene — fixed the recurring vitest concurrency flake. Symptom: full api suite ran 222-225/231 with 6-13 random failures per run; isolated module runs always 100% green. Root cause was NOT vitest parallelism per se — it was accumulated cruft in the dev DB from killed test runs (Ctrl-C / OOM / crashes) where`afterAll`cleanup didn't fire. Cruft like`T018-A1`vendor codes then collided with the next run's`beforeAll`inserts → ConflictError. New`apps/api/test/global-setup.ts`wires into vitest's`globalSetup`; runs once before any test file, deletes test-prefixed rows (`code LIKE 'T%-%'`) from all transactional + master tables in FK-safe order (NCs/DCs/GRNs/POs/PRs/SOs/JWs/JCs first, then items/vendors/clients/machines/operators); CASCADE handles lines + jc_ops + op_log + running_ops. Initial attempt with `pool: 'forks' + singleFork: true`made things worse — surfaced 13 failures from cruft instead of masking them with parallel afterAll cleanup. Reverted that, kept only the global setup. **Result: 3 consecutive full-suite runs returned 231/231 green, 230/231, 231/231** (1 transient — likely the residual v_jc_status snapshot race documented earlier in RUNBOOK). Massive improvement from 6-13 random fails to 0-1 per run. Total wall-time ~14s vs prior ~12s — cleanup adds 1-2s and does ~12 DELETE queries. The proper long-term fix per Phase 1/2 carry-over notes is a dedicated CI/staging Supabase project; until that lands, this keeps daily dev iteration smooth.)

- **BOM-8 cascade** (`apps/api/src/modules/bom-master/cascade.ts`) — `cascadeBomToSoLine(tx, soLineId, user)`: looks up the SO line's `sourceBomMasterId`, walks BOM lines, spawns child JC (manufacture, code `JC-BOM-<slug>-NN`, orderQty = soLineQty × qtyPerSet, sourceSoLineId = parent SO line so T-033 cascade still closes back) and child PR (purchase / outsource, code `PR-BOM-<slug>-NN`, vendor `'TBD'` placeholder, operation `'OUTSOURCE'` differentiates outsource from purchase). Idempotent: re-runs return `fired: false` and create nothing new (checked by source_so_line_id already-existing children). Emits `BOM_CASCADE` activity log row. **Hooked into** `createSalesOrder` so any line with `sourceBomMasterId` set triggers the cascade in the same tx as the SO insert (rollback unwinds cleanly).
- **Shared SO schemas extended** — `salesOrderLineInputSchema.sourceBomMasterId?` for writes, `salesOrderLineSchema.sourceBomMasterId` for reads (`null` default).
- **Excel import** (BOM-5) intentionally scoped to client-side parsing via the `xlsx` library — happens in the web forms (BOM-10), no server endpoint required since item-code resolution piggybacks on the existing /items query.

**Closed previous Active Task — ISSUE-007 fix:**
[Omitted long context line]
**Title:** Cascade sets `job_cards.closed_at` so the JC moves from `'complete'` to `'closed'` after sales-cascade
**Status:** [x] Code complete 2026-05-19.

**Done:**

- **Service (`apps/api/src/modules/op-entry/sales-cascade.ts`):** Inside `tryCascadeJcComplete`, after the inner cascadeSo / cascadeJw confirms a line was closed (and right before emitting `JC_COMPLETE`), update `job_cards.closed_at = now() WHERE id = jobCardId AND closed_at IS NULL` — idempotent via the IS NULL guard, in the same tx as the audit so rollback unwinds both. Early-return check at the top relaxed from `if (computedStatus !== 'complete')` to `if (computedStatus !== 'complete' && computedStatus !== 'closed')` so idempotent re-runs (after closed_at is set, view projects `'closed'` not `'complete'`) still flow through to the inner cascade and return the canonical `skipped: 'so_line_already_terminal'` instead of a misleading `skipped: 'jc_not_complete'`.
- **Tests:** 2 new in `sales-cascade.test.ts` — `ISSUE-007: cascade sets job_cards.closed_at when it closes the SO line` (verifies closed_at is null pre-cascade then Date post-cascade); `ISSUE-007: closed_at is idempotent — re-running cascade does NOT update it` (captures closed_at timestamp, re-runs `tryCascadeJcComplete`, asserts the timestamp is unchanged + skipped reason is `so_line_already_terminal`).
- **ISSUES.md:** ISSUE-007 row flipped `[ ] open` → `[x] Fixed 2026-05-19`.
- **Quality gates:** api typecheck + lint + prettier clean; 12/12 cascade tests green (was 10, +2 from this fix).

**Downstream impact:** `v_jc_status.computed_status` now projects `'closed'` for cascade-completed JCs (previously stuck at `'complete'`). Reports / alerts / dashboards keying off `closed_at` (jc-ageing report, al-012-jc-overdue alert, etc.) now see the JC as closed. The earlier ADR-026 view-update change for outsource ops is unaffected.

**Closed previous Active Task — T-042 (Partial — first slice):**
[Omitted long context line]
**Title:** Phase 7 — Materialize `v_item_stock` via trigger-maintained `item_stock_balances` table
**Status:** [x] Code complete 2026-05-19. DB + tests shipped in one session.

**Done:**

- **DB:** Migration `0020_phase7_item_stock_table.sql` — new `item_stock_balances (company_id, item_id, on_hand_qty, updated_at)` table with PK on (company_id, item_id), RLS company_isolation read policy (no write policy; only the trigger writes). AFTER INSERT trigger on `store_transactions` calls `apply_store_txn_to_balance()` (SECURITY DEFINER, bypasses RLS) which upserts the balance row by txn_type (`in` → +qty, `out` → -qty, `adjust` → +qty per the existing view convention). Backfill from current ledger via `INSERT … ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` so the table starts populated and the same statement doubles as a reconcile re-run. `v_item_stock` view rewritten to `SELECT * FROM item_stock_balances` — preserves the column contract so every existing caller (`getItemBalance`, qc-stock-cascade, GRN cascades, DC outward/cancel cascades, DC receipt cascades) works without code changes. Items FK has `ON DELETE CASCADE` so item hard-delete cleans the cache. Applied to dev via `_apply_0020.mjs`. Drizzle schema entry added for type safety.
- **Tests:** **8/8 green** in store-transactions suite (3 existing + 5 new T-042 trigger tests covering in-direction upsert, out-direction reduce, mixed in/out/adjust matches live SUM, item_id=NULL skipped no row, v_item_stock view returns same value as direct table read). **92/92 green** across dependent suites (GRN + DC + op-entry) — zero regression on cascading writes that depend on `v_item_stock` for stock_before reads.
- **Quality gates:** api typecheck + lint + prettier clean.

**Why a partial T-042:** Remaining candidates (materializing `v_jc_op_status` with refresh triggers, monthly NC / op-log aggregate views) all add refresh-trigger complexity for unclear leverage at our 1–2 user scale. Deferred until production perf data exists post-Phase 9 cutover; T-042 row flips `[ ]` → `[~] Partial` rather than `[x] Done`.

**Read-cost impact:** `v_item_stock` queries dropped from `SUM(N store_txns)` (full table scan filtered by company+item) to single-row PK lookup. Hottest callers — QC accept cascade (T-040f), JW DC issue (T-059a), JW DC receive (T-059b), GRN QC accept (T-036c) — all now read stock_before in O(1) instead of O(N).

**Closed previous Active Task — T-059b (Phase 6 — Outsource DC receive-back):**
[Omitted long context line]
**Title:** Phase 6 — Outsource DC receive-back (closes ISSUE-003 fully)
**Status:** [x] Code complete 2026-05-19. API + web both shipped in one session per ADR-026.

**Done:**

- **DB:** Migration `0019_phase6_dc_receipts.sql` — 2 new tables (`delivery_challan_receipts` header + `delivery_challan_receipt_lines` per-line received + rejected qty) with `ON DELETE CASCADE` from both parent (DC for header, dc_line for receipt_line) so admin purges + test cleanup don't orphan. CHECK constraints enforce non-negative qtys, positive sum, and required `reject_reason` when `rejected_qty > 0` (mirrored by a Zod refine on the input schema so client UX surfaces the error before insert). `v_jc_op_status` view replaced (DROP + CREATE; `v_jc_status` re-created identically since it depends on the op view): new `outsource_receipts_rollup` CTE joins receipt_lines through dc_lines (by `purchase_order_line_id`) excluding cancelled / deleted DCs; `prev_output` CTE uses `received - rejected` for outsource ops (fixes the latent bug where outsource ops projected 0 prev_output to next op since `completed_qty` is always 0 for them); new `WHEN op_type='outsource' AND outsource_status='received' THEN 'complete'` clause makes `v_jc_status.done_ops` count fully-received outsource ops so the sales-cascade fires when outsource is the last/only op of a JC. Applied to dev via `_apply_0019.mjs` (DLP-friendly inlined applier — same pattern as 0016/0018). Drizzle schema updated.
- **Shared:** `packages/shared/src/schemas/delivery-challan.ts` extended with `createDeliveryChallanReceiptInputSchema` + `createDeliveryChallanReceiptLineInputSchema` (with Zod refines for positive-sum + reject-reason required), `deliveryChallanReceiptSchema` + `deliveryChallanReceiptLineSchema` read shapes. `deliveryChallanWithLinesSchema.extend({ receipts: ... })` so the detail load bundles receipts.
- **Cascade helpers:** new `apps/api/src/modules/delivery-challans/receipt-cascades.ts` — `applyReceiveToJcOp` (sums cumulative received+rejected qty per PO line via SQL; flips `outsource_status: sent → received` when reconciled, no-op otherwise), `writeStoreTxnOnDcReceive` (txn_type=in, source_type=jw_in; locks items row FOR UPDATE; rejected qty does NOT credit stock — only good received qty does), `autoCreateNcFromOutsourceReject` (mirrors T-040e's `autoCreateNcFromQcReject` pattern; generates `NC-AUTO-<jcCode>-Op<N>-OS-<HHMMSSmmm>` with 3-attempt collision retry + reason_category='other' since NC enum has no outsource bucket — detail string carries the source), `isDcFullyReconciled` (SQL helper checking all outward lines fully covered by active receipts), `dcHasActiveReceipts` (guard for cancel block).
- **Service:** `receiveAgainstDeliveryChallan(deliveryChallanId, input, user)` in `apps/api/src/modules/delivery-challans/service.ts`. Inside `withUserContext`: validates DC not cancelled / not already fully received, validates every input line belongs to this DC (ValidationError), checks cumulative received+rejected per line ≤ sent_qty (ConflictError), generates auto-receipt code `RCPT-<dcCode>-NN` (sequence per DC, idempotent via dup-check loop with 5 attempts), inserts header + lines, writes stock IN per receipt line (good qty only), groups per-po-line aggregates to call `applyReceiveToJcOp` once per po_line, fires `autoCreateNcFromOutsourceReject` per receipt line with `rejected_qty > 0` (looks up the jc_op via raw SQL since multiple receipt lines may target the same po_line), flips DC status `issued → received` only when ALL outward lines fully reconciled, emits `DC_RECEIVE` / `OP_OUTSOURCE_RECEIVED` (only on full receive of a given op) / `DC_COMPLETE` audit rows, and calls `tryCascadeJcComplete(jobCardId, user)` from `op-entry/sales-cascade.ts` for every JC whose outsource op just flipped fully-received — same tx, so a cascade failure rolls back the whole receipt. `cancelDeliveryChallan` extended with a new guard: refuses cancel once receipts exist (ConflictError "DC has receipts; cancel until receipts are voided") since reversing receipts cleanly (unwind stock IN, void auto-NC, restore JC status) is out of scope for this slice. `loadDeliveryChallanWithLines` extended to also load receipts + their lines (one extra round-trip on detail; ordered by `receipt_date, receipt_code`).
- **Routes:** `POST /delivery-challans/:id/receive` (201) — parses receipt input via shared Zod schema; service returns DC detail bundle with the new receipt embedded.
- **Tests:** **39/39 green** in DC suite (24 service + 15 routes, was 22 with +17 from T-059b). New under T-059b: 12 service tests covering full receive flow + partial receive + cumulative across 2 receipts + over-receive 409 + reject-qty auto-NC + reject-reason-missing rejected by Zod + stock_txn shape + audit rows + sales-cascade from outsource-only JC + viewer 403 + DC 404 + cancelled-DC 409 + wrong-DC-line ValidationError + cancel-after-receipt block; 3 route tests covering 201 receive + viewer 403 + reject-missing-reason 400.
- **Web:** `useReceiveDeliveryChallan` hook in `api.ts`. New `routes/receive.tsx` — receive form: loads parent DC, prefills per-line drafts with `sent / already_received / remaining` computed from `detail.receipts`, per-line inputs for received_qty + rejected_qty + reject_reason (reason required + autofocused when rejected_qty > 0), receipt header (receipt_date + vendor_invoice + remarks), submit validates client-side then calls the API. Detail page extended with: a "Receive" button next to "Cancel DC" (admin/manager only, only when status='issued'); a per-line aggregate of received + rejected qty pulled from the receipts payload; a new "Receipts" section listing each receipt as a sub-card with line-level breakdown (DC line ref + received + rejected + reject_reason + remarks). Web route registered in `router.tsx`.
- **Quality gates:** api typecheck + lint + prettier + 39/39 DC tests green; web typecheck + lint + prettier + build clean (2289 modules, 5.70s, index 999.76 KB raw / 132.19 KB gzip — still under 1000 KB ceiling). Global-setup wipe extended to handle `delivery_challan_receipts` by code prefix + `nc_register` `NC-AUTO-T%` codes (auto-NCs against T-prefixed JCs were leaking past the prior `T%-%` filter, breaking job_cards cleanup with FK violations).

**What this unblocks:** ISSUE-003 fully. The full sales cascade chain on migrated data: `IN-JC-00002` op 7 (COATING outsource) can now go `sent → received` via the new receive flow, which flips the jc_op's `computed_status` to `'complete'` via the patched view, which (when QC ops 8/9 are also resolved via T-040d) drives `v_jc_status.computed_status='complete'`, which fires the JC→SO-line cascade onto `SO-436 line 6`.

**Closed previous Active Task — T-059a (Phase 6 — Outsource DC outward create + cancel):**
[Omitted long context line]
**Title:** Phase 6 — Outsource DC outward create + cancel (closes ISSUE-003 outward half)
**Status:** [x] Code complete 2026-05-18. API + web both shipped in one session per ADR-026.

**Done:**

- **DB:** Migration `0018_phase6_dc_po_line_link.sql` (one new column `purchase_order_line_id` on `delivery_challan_lines` + FK + index; nullable so non-JW DCs still work). Applied to dev via `_apply_0018.mjs` (DLP-friendly inlined applier — same workaround used for 0016 alerts migration). Drizzle schema updated.
- **Shared:** `packages/shared/src/schemas/delivery-challan.ts` extended with `createDeliveryChallanInputSchema` + `createDeliveryChallanLineInputSchema`. `purchaseOrderLineId` added to read shape.
- **Cascade helpers:** new `apps/api/src/modules/delivery-challans/cascades.ts` — `applyOutwardToJcOp` (bumps `outsource_sent_qty`, sets `outsource_sent_date`/`outsource_dc_no`, transitions `outsource_status: po_created/pr_raised/pending → sent`), `reverseOutwardFromJcOp` (cancel-path inverse with status downgrade only when sent_qty hits 0), `writeStoreTxnOnDcIssue` (txn_type=out, source_type=jw_out, locks items row FOR UPDATE), `reverseStoreTxnOnDcCancel` (compensating IN row with same source_type, marked "(cancel)").
- **Service:** `createDeliveryChallan` + `cancelDeliveryChallan` in `apps/api/src/modules/delivery-challans/service.ts`. Both run inside `withUserContext`; cascades fire in the same tx so rollbacks unwind cleanly. Create validates qty ≤ `po_line.qty - already_sent_across_active_dcs` per PO line, rejects duplicate code, denies viewer. Cancel is admin-only (manager → 403), rejects already-cancelled / already-received with `ConflictError`. Both emit audit rows: `DC_ISSUE` / `OP_OUTSOURCE_SENT` on create; `DC_CANCEL` / `OP_OUTSOURCE_REVERSED` on cancel. **Refactor:** extracted `loadDeliveryChallanWithLines(tx, id, companyId)` helper so the write services return the freshly-inserted row from inside the open tx instead of opening a nested `withUserContext` (which broke due to pool isolation — surfaced as `NotFoundError` on every create test until extracted).
- **Routes:** `POST /delivery-challans` (201) + `POST /delivery-challans/:id/cancel` (200).
- **Tests:** **22/22 green** in DC suite (16 service + 6 routes). New under T-059a:
  - 11 service tests — happy create + jc_op flip + stock OUT + audit rows + qty exceed → 409 + duplicate code → 409 + viewer → 403 + cancel reverse + manager → 403 + unknown id → 404 + idempotent cancel → 409.
  - 3 routes tests — POST 201, POST :id/cancel 200, viewer POST → 403.
- **Web:** `useCreateDeliveryChallan` + `useCancelDeliveryChallan` hooks in `api.ts`. New `routes/create.tsx` (wizard: `?poId=<id>` loads PO → prefills line drafts with `purchase_order_line_id` + item + PO qty, user enters ship qty per line, submit). "New DC" button on list page; "Cancel DC" button on detail (admin-only, status='issued'). "Issue DC" button on PO detail (replaces "Receive (new GRN)" when `po.poType === 'job_work'`).
- **Quality gates:** api typecheck + lint + prettier clean; web typecheck + lint + prettier + build clean (2288 modules, 5.96s, index 974 KB raw / 129 KB gzip — still under 1000 KB ceiling).

**What this unblocks:** ISSUE-003 outward half. The cascade for `IN-JC-00002` op 7 (COATING outsource) can now be driven through to `'sent'` state via the new DC outward flow. Full e2e cascade against migrated data still requires the receive-back flow (T-059b) — once that ships, `IN-JC-00002` → `SO-436 line 6` cascade can be driven end-to-end through real UI.

**Out of scope (deferred to T-059b):**

- Receive-back flow (`delivery_challan_receipts` table + `receiveAgainstDeliveryChallan` service + auto-NC on reject + `v_jc_op_status` update so received outsource ops project `complete` for sales-cascade).
- PO line `received_qty` rollup for JW POs (currently 0; derivable from DC receipts join).
- PDF print templates (Phase 7 T-041e UX-deferred).
- `partyMaterials` deduction (doc_missing per ADR-017 / ADR-023).

**Closed previous Active Task — T-040g (Phase 6 — QC engineer dashboard):**

[x] Code complete 2026-05-16. Worked around for 0016 by inlining the SQL as a TS literal array in a one-off `_apply_0016.ts` script. Permanent fix candidate: rewrite `apply-sql.ts` with a leaner statement iterator OR rename .sql files to a non-flagged extension. Also: the standard `pnpm --filter api test` invocation buffers under DLP — `node --env-file=../../.env.local node_modules/vitest/vitest.mjs run <pattern>` from `apps/api` is the working alternative and streams output cleanly.

## Closed — T-059 (Railway prod CORS unblock)

**ID:** T-059
**Title:** Unblock Railway prod by setting `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` (or relaxing cors.ts)
**Status:** [x] Done (2026-05-09) — Path 1 chosen: `ALLOWED_ORIGINS=https://innovic-erp.pages.dev` set in Railway api service Variables tab as a placeholder (Cloudflare Pages frontend not deployed yet — value replaces with the real prod hostname when that lands). Railway auto-redeployed; deploy went green; the 9 queued commits (`e94453e..80688b6`) all activated. `/health` confirmed 200 (liveness, no DB call); `/readyz` confirmed 200 + `db:"up"` after pool warm. RUNBOOK "Verify health" subsection updated to reflect the actual two-endpoint split that's been live since `80688b6`.

**Symptoms (from Railway dashboard screenshots `E:/AI trails/ERP supa/ER1_08-05-26*.jpg`):** every deploy from `e94453e` (2026-05-07) onward shows "Deployment failed during network process" → "Healthcheck failure" at the Network/Healthcheck stage. 9 consecutive failures: `e94453e e4b116d-as-removed 6bf88b8 946a83c ce99dcb 6aba991 d561eb2 34a3255 0ed30e9 a9161b8 491a92d 80688b6`. Build + Deploy stages succeed; only Healthcheck fails after 53s. `dad41a52` is Railway's deploy hash for the latest attempt (`80688b6`).

**Initial misdiagnosis:** thought `/health` was timing out on the DB ping (2s timeout, cold-start TLS to Supabase Mumbai exceeds it). Shipped commit `80688b6` splitting `/health` (always-200 liveness) from `/readyz` (DB-aware) + bumping pingDatabase default to 8s. Did NOT fix the deploy. The api never got far enough to register `/health` at all.

**Real cause:** `apps/api/src/lib/cors.ts:19-22` throws an Error in `resolveCorsOriginFrom()` when `NODE_ENV=production` AND `opts.allowedOrigins.length === 0`. Called during `app.register(cors, { origin: resolveCorsOrigin() })` at boot. When Railway has `NODE_ENV=production` (it does — visible in the 7 vars panel) but no `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` set, the throw fires inside the CORS plugin's `register()`, the api process crashes before `app.listen()`, no socket binds, Railway's healthcheck cannot reach `/health` (or any endpoint), Railway interprets that as "Healthcheck failure". This was introduced in commit `e94453e` ("tighten CORS to env-driven allowlist") on 2026-05-07 — the EXACT moment the failure pattern starts in the dashboard timeline.

**Acceptance:**

- [ ] Railway prod redeploys successfully on next push to `main`
- [ ] Production reflects the latest commit (T-041d Phase A alerts module visible in browser)
- [ ] `/health` returns 200 with no DB call; `/readyz` returns 200 + `db: up` after pool warms

**Two unblock paths (offered to user 2026-05-08, deferred to next session):**

1. **(Recommended)** Set `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` in Railway api service → Variables tab. Value = production frontend URL (Cloudflare Pages — exact URL TBD; ask user). Format = comma-separated list. Save → Railway auto-redeploys. The strict-CORS protection stays intact, which is the original ADR intent.
2. Relax `apps/api/src/lib/cors.ts` to `logger.warn(...)` + return permissive `true` instead of throwing in production. Loses the safety check that catches this exact misconfiguration. Faster to unblock but a security regression.
3. Both: set the env var AND also relax cors.ts to warn-don't-throw for double safety.

**Notes for next session:**

- 9 commits queued: `git log e94453e..HEAD` lists them all.
- The fix in commit `80688b6` (`/health` liveness/readiness split + 8s timeout) is correct independently — keep it. It just wasn't the only blocker.
- After Railway is unblocked, T-041d slice 6 is the next implementation: alert_subscriptions table + alert_deliveries audit table + migration + apply + service + routes + BullMQ worker processor + idempotency on (alert_code, user_id, window_start) + web subscription UI on dashboard rows. ADR-024 already documents the design.
- Then slice 7: RUNBOOK setup steps for Redis + Resend, TASKS.md sign-off.

## Deferred Task — T-046 (Phase 8 design tracker)

**Status:** [-] Deferred 2026-05-06 per ADR-022

**Why:** All 8 legacy design collections are `doc_missing` (zero rows ever written by legacy app):

- System v2: `designProjects`, `designTasks`, `designIssues`, `designWorkLog`, `designDCRs`, `designDCNs` (project-task-issue tree with change-control, legacy HTML L7531-7651, `DP-NNNN`)
- System v1: `designTracker`, `designTimeLog` (flat per-SO tracker used by `_canStartProductionForSO` gate, legacy HTML L7485-7486, `DSN-NNNN`)

Building 4 tables now would require designing in a vacuum AND picking between two competing legacy specs with no UX requirements driving the choice. Same pitfall ADR-016 §"Alternatives Considered → A" rejected for `qc_inspections`, and ADR-017 §1 rejected for the 8 dispatch / JW DC / party / OSP / store-issue collections. ADR-022 applies the precedent uniformly: doc_missing modules wait for real workflow requirements before schema design starts.

**When to revisit:** when a designer or PM brings actual UX requirements ("here's what design tracking needs to do for our shop"), at which point the schema gets designed forward against those requirements rather than backward from legacy code. Legacy spec source (`legacy/InnovicERP_v82_12_3_DataLossFix_29-04-2026.html`) and exports (`migration/export/design*.json`) remain available as design inspiration, not as a binding spec.

**Forward-looking finding (acted on 2026-05-06 same day via ADR-023):** T-047 / T-048 / T-049 / T-050 batch-deferred — see section below.

**delivery-challans** is read-only by design — service has only `listDeliveryChallans` + `getDeliveryChallan`; no service-layer mutators exist yet, so emitter wiring deferred until the DC mutation surface ships in a future task.

**Deferred follow-ons:**

- **Finer-grained QC_ACCEPT / QC_REJECT** on GRN per-line state transitions (currently folded into EDIT) — only worth it if the audit feed actually needs that resolution.
- **DC emitter** once the DC mutation flow ships.

## Closed Task — T-041b

**ID:** T-041b
**Title:** Phase 7 — drag-and-drop ad-hoc report builder
**Status:** [x] Done (2026-05-05)
**Scope:**

- Layered on T-041a engine — saved report = `AdHocSpec` jsonb stored in new `saved_reports` table; runner translates spec → safe parameterised SQL via a whitelisted source catalog
- 5 sources for v1: sales-orders, purchase-orders, job-cards, items-stock, nc-register (covers 5 of legacy's 13 `_rbSources`; the rest are doc_missing per ADR-016/-017 or future-phase)
- Native HTML5 drag & drop UI mirrors legacy `renderReportBuilder` (legacy HTML L17434+) — Available fields → Columns/Filters/Group-By zones, inline filter op + value editor, optional Group-By + sumCol + sumFn picker (SUM/COUNT/AVG/MIN/MAX)
- Shared/private toggle — shared reports visible to everyone in the company; only owner or admin/manager can edit. Per-user gate enforced at the service layer; RLS does company isolation only
- 8 endpoints under `/saved-reports/*` (sources, list, create, get, update, delete, run, preview)
- ADR-018 documents the design tradeoffs (why declarative spec over arbitrary SQL, why catalog in shared, why service-layer enforcement of shared/private vs an `current_user_id()` SQL helper)

**Acceptance:**

- [x] `saved_reports` table + migrations applied; standard company_isolation RLS; service-layer ownership gate
- [x] `runner.assertSpec` rejects unknown columns, incompatible op/type, mismatched sumCol type
- [x] All filter values bound via Drizzle's parameterised sql template; identifiers via `sql.identifier()`
- [x] `GET /saved-reports/:id/run` + `POST /saved-reports/preview` both run inside `withUserContext`
- [x] Web builder mirrors legacy zones; live preview; CSV export; shared/private badge in list
- [x] api suite 259/259 green (was 231, +28); workspace typecheck + lint + format clean; web build clean

## Closed Task — T-040b

**ID:** T-040b
**Title:** Phase 6 — NC disposition workflow + service-layer cascades
**Status:** [x] Done (2026-05-04)
**Scope:**

- Implement legacy `_disposeNC` behaviour (legacy line 22618) as a service-layer action (`disposeNc(id, action, ...)`) with cascades. Action enum mirrors the disposition enum: `rework` / `scrap` / `use_as_is` / `return_to_vendor` / `make_fresh`.
- **Cascade matrix (legacy):**
  - `rework` → flip status to `disposed`, write disposition fields, increment `jc_ops.reworkQty` for the picked rework op (`reworkOpSeq`). NC stays `disposed` until `closeNcRework(id)` action flips to `closed`.
  - `scrap` → flip status to `closed`, set `scrap_cost` from input, no other cascade.
  - `use_as_is` → flip status to `closed`, append an `op_log` row with `type='qc'`, qty = rejected_qty, remarks = `'Use As Is — from <ncCode> (<n> pcs accepted with concession)'`. Mirrors legacy line 22669-22674.
  - `return_to_vendor` → flip status to `closed`, no other cascade.
  - `make_fresh` → flip status to `closed`, create supplementary JC (copy from origin JC's source link, qty = rejected, status = `open`, remarks = `'Supplementary for <ncCode> — replace rejected <n> pcs'`), set `rework_jc_code_text` to the new JC code. Mirrors legacy line 22682-22692.
- All cascades run in the same DB tx as the NC update; rollback unwinds cleanly. Same shape as T-036c GRN-QC-write cascade.
- Auto-NC-from-QC-call shortcut (legacy `_autoCreateNC`) — service action callable from op-entry that creates an NC against a JC op when QC rejects.
- 1-2 day scope; pure service + tests + UI buttons (no schema changes).

**Acceptance:**

- [ ] `disposeNc` service action covers all 5 dispositions with cascades + transactional rollback; tests cover each path including the supplementary-JC creation
- [ ] `closeNcRework` service action flips `disposed` (rework path) → `closed` after rework qty captured
- [ ] Web NC detail page surfaces the dispose button (admin/manager/qc/operator) when status=`pending`; shows the close-rework button when status=`disposed` AND disposition=`rework`
- [ ] Op-entry web flow gets a "Report NC" shortcut on the JC-op row that pre-fills the form
- [ ] api suite green; web build clean; browser smoke gated on user

## Policy questions to resolve before T-040b starts

1. **Which role can dispose?** Legacy `canEntry()` includes admin/manager/operator (no separate `qc` role exists today). Recommended: same set, with optional QC-role pickup if/when seeded. Or restrict to admin/manager only (operators report NCs but don't disposition them)?
2. **Auto-CAPA threshold?** Legacy lets users manually create CAPA from any closed NC. Should some dispositions auto-create CAPA (e.g. all `scrap` ones)? Or stay manual via a button on the NC detail page?
3. **Supplementary JC's source FK?** Make-Fresh creates a new JC. Should it inherit the original JC's `source_so_line_id` / `source_jw_line_id`, or have a `parent_nc_id` link instead, or both?
4. **Rework qty interaction with existing planned-vs-actual model?** `jc_ops.reworkQty` is currently a column with no application use yet (legacy migrated as-is). When dispose-Rework increments it, does the JC's planned vs available calc need to account for it (so operators see "12 pieces required, 5 in rework pool")? Or stay as a passive audit column for now?
5. **Use-As-Is op_log row's source attribution?** Legacy writes `operator: currentUser().name`. Should ours write the disposition_by user as the operator, or leave operator NULL with a note in remarks?

## T-040a closure summary (2026-05-04)

- 1 hand-written policy migration (operator-write on nc_register), 2 new shared schemas, 2 new api modules (NC: full CRUD; DC: read-only) with 23 tests, 2 new web modules with home nav cards. api suite 198/198 green; workspace lint + typecheck + web build clean. Browser smoke gated on user.

## T-030 browser smoke checklist (run in dev, 5–10 min)

1. `pnpm --filter web dev` (separate terminal: `pnpm --filter api dev`)
2. Sign in → home → "Sales orders" card visible (Cog/ClipboardList icon)
3. List: 2 SOs visible (`SO-DEMO-EQ`, `SO-436`); search/status/type filters work; pagination if more than 25 (currently won't trigger)
4. Detail: click `SO-436` → 8 lines render, total qty in header card = 494
5. Edit existing SO: change a line qty, remove one line, add a new line → save → redirects to detail; verify the absent line is gone (it was soft-deleted) and the new line appears with the next sequential lineNo
6. New SO: fill header (auto-pre-filled SO No is fine) + 1 line → save → redirects to detail
7. Sign out, sign in as a `viewer` user (if seeded) → list works, edit/new buttons might still render (RLS check is at API), but POST returns 403 → toast surfaces
8. Soft-spot: edit an existing SO without retyping any line item codes → confirm save succeeds (the form's hidden `itemId` preservation is what makes this work)
9. Soft-spot: confirm `gstPercent` re-binds correctly when editing an SO whose `gstPercent="18.00"` — the Select should default to 18%, not blank

## Phase 3 carry-over notes (open questions to resolve in T-024a schema design)

- **`routeCards` (legacy collection, 14 records exported)** is in the Phase 1 export but NOT in CLAUDE.md §13 glossary or `docs/SCHEMA.md` Module map. Decide in T-024a: separate `route_cards` master table (linked to items via item-id) OR denormalised onto `job_cards` as a snapshot at JC-creation time. Quote the legacy HTML usage (`legacy/InnovicERP_v82_12_3_DataLossFix_29-04-2026.html`) before deciding. Record decision as an ADR.
- **Status enums must reflect ALL legacy values, not just exhibited ones.** Source data is small (3 + 20 + 81 = 104 rows) — easy to design a schema that fits the export but breaks on a status the data didn't happen to hit. Read the legacy HTML's status-handling JS for `jobCards`, `jcOps`, `opLog` and capture every literal status string before locking the enum.
- **Quantity columns:** `jc_ops` and `op_log` need planned-vs-actual qty modelling. The "cannot exceed planned qty" / "cannot skip required QC" validations from T-026 hinge on this. Pin column names + types in T-024a; don't punt.
- **`runningOps` (legacy collection, 2 records exported)** likely materialises live op-entry state. Decide in T-024a: is this a derived view over `op_log` OR a real table? Probably a view if we're doing optimistic updates via TanStack Query.
- **Realtime selectivity** (ADR-004): `op_log` IS one of the four hot screens, so the table needs to support filtered Postgres Realtime subs. Confirm column shape supports the planned filter (most likely `(company_id, jc_op_id)` row filter).

## Phase 2 carry-over notes (from Phase 1 sign-off)

- ~~**CORS currently permissive** (`origin: true, credentials: true` in `apps/api/src/server.ts`). Acceptable while web is local-only; **tighten to a specific allowlist before Cloudflare Pages web deploy** is wired.~~ **Resolved 2026-05-07.** New `ALLOWED_ORIGINS` env var (comma-separated list) parsed in `apps/api/src/lib/env.ts`; `apps/api/src/lib/cors.ts` exports `resolveCorsOrigin()` that returns the explicit list, falls back to permissive `origin: true` + warning in dev/test when unset, and **throws** in production when unset (API refuses to start). Documented in RUNBOOK.md "Required env vars" + new `.env.example` entry seeded with `http://localhost:5173,http://127.0.0.1:5173` for dev.
- **CI tests reuse dev Supabase secrets.** Tests prefix-isolate (`T009R-`) and clean up after themselves so this is safe at current scale, but **provision a separate CI/staging Supabase project before Phase 4** (sales chain) — test data volume + concurrency will grow.
- ~~Smoke session behaviour to confirm in Phase 2 — viewer write response shape.~~ **Resolved 2026-05-01.** Code analysis confirmed the leak (every service had only `requireCompany`, no role check; RLS would block but the error handler fall-through returns generic 500). Fixed via `apps/api/src/lib/auth.ts:requireWriteRole` called at top of every `create`/`update`/`softDelete` across all 5 master modules. Regression test in `items/routes.test.ts` asserts viewer → 403 `{error: "forbidden"}`. Full api suite green at 57/57.
- ~~**`pnpm format` not yet run workspace-wide** (T-010c). Re-enable `format:check` in `ci.yml` once formatting is normalised.~~ **Resolved 2026-05-04.** Ran `pnpm format` workspace-wide; new `.prettierignore` excludes drizzle-generated snapshots + migration pipeline artifacts. Added `Format check` step to `lint-typecheck` job in `ci.yml`. 180 files reformatted (pure whitespace/quote/wrap churn); api 209/209 green, migration 137/137 green.

| 2026-05-04 | Web bundle split                            | **Web bundle code-split — 1 chunk → 6 chunks via `manualChunks`.** Build was emitting a "chunk larger than 500 kB" warning on every CI run + every local build because all 1938 modules collapsed into a single 1,649 KB / 357 KB gzip JS file. Added a `splitVendorChunk(id)` function in `apps/web/vite.config.ts` that routes node_modules deps to named vendor chunks based on path: `@tanstack/*` → `vendor-tanstack` (283 KB / 85 KB gzip; router + query + table); `lucide-react` → `vendor-icons` (13 KB / 3 KB gzip — note: tree-shaking already does most of the work since we import individual icons); `@supabase/*` → `vendor-supabase` (206 KB / 53 KB gzip — Supabase client + transitive deps); `react-hook-form` / `@hookform/*` / `/zod/` → `vendor-forms` (87 KB / 24 KB gzip); `/react/` / `/react-dom/` / `/scheduler/` → `vendor-react` (341 KB / 102 KB gzip); everything else (small utils — clsx, cva, tw-merge, zustand, @radix-ui/react-slot, tailwind-merge, etc.) stays in the main app `index` chunk. App `index` lands at 777 KB / 101 KB gzip — that's app code + the small utils + the in-tree shared package. `chunkSizeWarningLimit` bumped to 1000 KB inline-justified comment (the gzip footprint is what users actually download; an SPA with 4 list/detail/new/edit screens × 15 modules is genuinely ~100 KB gzip + framework). Cache benefit on deploys: when a service ships a new version, the user only re-downloads the app `index` chunk + maybe one vendor chunk if a dep bumped — not the entire 1.65 MB. **Build clean, no warning, 3.65s.** Workspace typecheck + lint clean. | 2026-05-04 | T-040b                                      | **Phase 6 NC disposition workflow + service-layer cascades shipped.** All 5 policy questions answered with the recommended defaults at the start of the task. (1) **Dispose role = admin/manager/operator** — matches T-040a's `entry_write` RLS policy + service uses `requireOpEntryRole`. (2) **Auto-CAPA = manual button only** — CAPA records are doc_missing per ADR-017 so auto-creating into a fresh schema is premature; a manual CAPA button can land in T-040c. (3) **Supplementary JC inheritance = source SO/JW link + new `parent_nc_id` FK on job_cards** — preserves T-033 close cascade so completing the supp JC still closes the SO line; parent_nc_id makes "all supp JCs from this NC" a single query. New schema alter `0012_phase6_jc_parent_nc.sql` (drizzle-gen) + partial index `job_cards_parent_nc_idx`; FK is `ON DELETE SET NULL` so dropping the NC doesn't cascade-delete supp JCs (manufacturing audit needs them). (4) **Rework qty interaction = passive audit only** — `jc_ops.rework_qty` continues to live as a column but op-entry available-qty calc is NOT re-routed through it; defer until shop-floor reports actual confusion (ADR-016/-017 / CLAUDE.md §6 #6 spirit). (5) **Use-As-Is op_log operator attribution = byName lookup with NULL+remarks fallback** — preserves audit trail; legacy `currentUser().name` semantics. New `cascades.ts` module (~350 LOC, mirrors T-036c GRN cascade structure for testability) with 5 disposition paths: **rework** (re-reads NC inside tx, validates rework_op_seq exists on JC, bumps `jc_ops.rework_qty` by `rejected_qty`, flips status→disposed), **scrap** (clamps scrap_cost to ≥0, status→closed), **use_as_is** (validates NC has op_seq + jc_op_id, resolves operator via case-insensitive name match against operators master, appends `op_log` row with `log_type='qc'` + `qty=rejected_qty` + remarks pointing at the NC code, status→closed), **return_to_vendor** (status→closed, no side effects), **make_fresh** (re-reads origin JC, generates `<originCode>-S<n>` code by scanning existing supp JCs, inherits source_so_line_id/source_jw_line_id/source_legacy_ref, sets parent_nc_id, status→closed, stores new JC code in `rework_jc_code_text`). All cascades transactional; rollbacks unwind cleanly. New `closeNcReworkCascade` flips disposed+rework → closed and optionally captures `rework_done_qty`. 2 new service actions (`disposeNcRegister` resolves user-name from email's local-part + delegates to cascade; `closeNcRework` same shape). 2 new routes (`POST /nc-register/:id/dispose`, `POST /nc-register/:id/close-rework`). 11 new tests in `cascades.test.ts` covering all 5 dispositions + concurrent-dispose ConflictError + rework with explicit op_seq + rework default-to-NC.opSeq + bad-op-seq ValidationError + scrap cost capture + use-as-is op_log content + return-to-vendor zero side effects + make_fresh with `-S1`/`-S2` numbering + parent_nc_id wiring + use-as-is requires-jc-op-id ValidationError + close-rework happy path + close-rework wrong-disposition ConflictError. **api suite 209/209 green** (was 198, +11). Close-rework button (status=disposed + disposition=rework) with optional rework_done_qty input next to the button. Cascade fanout invalidates op-entry + job-cards caches on dispose so the UI refreshes (rework→jc_ops.rework_qty change visible; make_fresh→new JC visible in JC list). FOR UPDATE`lock so concurrent QC accepts on the same item serialize. | 2026-05-02 | T-033                                       | **SO/JW line + header auto-close cascade live.** New `apps/api/src/modules/op-entry/sales-cascade.ts` with `tryCascadeJcComplete(tx, jobCardId, user)`. Trigger: keyed off `v_jc_status.computed_status === 'complete'` (the canonical signal — fires on EVERY completion path that brings the JC to fully done, fixing the legacy `_autoCloseSO()` line 1355 bug where it only fired on the explicit Submit-Complete path). Wired into `submitOpLog` after the existing `available === 0` block (running_op auto-close + qcCallDate auto-set), inside the same Drizzle transaction. Logic: if JC is `complete` AND has source_so_line_id → flip line `open → closed`; if all sibling lines on the SO are now terminal (`closed` or `cancelled`), flip SO header `open → closed`. Same path for JW. Idempotent: rows already in `closed` or `cancelled` short-circuit with `{skipped: 'so_line_already_terminal'}` and don't re-write `updated_at`. **7 new cascade tests** (`sales-cascade.test.ts`): SO single-line line+header close, SO multi-line gradual close (line 1 closes alone → line 2 also closes → header), partial completion (2 ops, only op 1 done) doesn't cascade, idempotency (direct re-call is no-op), cancelled sibling (counts as terminal but isn't re-flipped), JW path parity, source-less JC (no error). Full api suite **120/120 green** (was 113, +7). Workspace typecheck + lint clean.
